1 int
2 de
3 param area
M: f: 1 auto
2 dir
3 trig
4 sub
Met 1/2 n/p: Method: Integration by substitution
1. u = 3*x + 1/3*pi
2. du/dx = 3
3. du = 3 dx
4. I = Int[1/3*sin(u)^2*cos(u)^2] du
5. = -1/32*sin(4*u) + 1/8*u + C
6. Substitute back u = 3*x + 1/3*pi.

8. Simplify.
= -1/32*sin(12*x + 4/3*pi) + 3/8*x + 1/24*pi + C

7. = -1/32*sin(4*(6*x - 1/6*pi)) + 1/8*(6*x - 1/6*pi) + C
8. Simplify.
= -1/32*sin(24*x - 2/3*pi) + 3/4*x - 1/48*pi + C
